Lines 51-70: `establishNewStream()` creates new bidirectional stream to management server\\n  - Line 74: `sendMessage()` sends DiscoveryRequest to server\\n  - Handles both SOTW (`DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse`) and Delta (`DeltaDiscoveryRequest/DeltaDiscoveryResponse`) variants\\n\\n## Configuration Flow Sequence\\n\\n1. **Envoy Startup**: Envoy creates a GrpcSubscriptionImpl for each xDS resource type (listeners, clusters, routes, etc.)\\n2. **Subscription Registration**: GrpcSubscriptionImpl calls `GrpcMux::addWatch()` to register interest in resources\\n3. **Stream Establishment**: GrpcMux creates a GrpcStream that establishes a bidirectional gRPC connection to the management server using the AggregatedDiscoveryService/StreamAggregatedResources RPC\\n4. **Request Sending**: Envoy sends DiscoveryRequest messages containing:\\n   - version_info: Current known version (empty on first request)\\n   - type_url: The resource type being requested (e.g., type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.v3.Listener)\\n   - resource_names: Specific resource names to subscribe to\\n   - response_nonce: For ACK/NACK responses\\n5. **Server Processing**: The control plane server (go-control-plane) receives the request in StreamAggregatedResources() handler\\n6. **Response Sending**: Server sends DiscoveryResponse with:\\n   - version_info: New configuration version\\n   - resources: Serialized protobuf resources\\n   - type_url: Matching the request\\n   - nonce: For pairing with subsequent ACK/NACK\\n7. **Configuration Update**: Envoy processes DiscoveryResponse, validates config, and either ACKs (sends new request with same version_info and nonce) or NACKs (sends error_detail)\\n8. **Stream Lifecycle**: The gRPC stream remains open, allowing push-based updates. If connection fails, GrpcStream automatically reconnects using backoff strategy\\n\\n## Delta xDS Variant\\n\\nFor resource-efficient updates, the Delta xDS variant uses:\\n- `DeltaDiscoveryRequest`: Includes only changed resources and removals\\n- `DeltaDiscoveryResponse`: Includes only delta resources and nonce (required for acknowledgment)\\n- Implemented in parallel infrastructure: `DeltaAggregatedResources` RPC in `ads.proto`\\n- Delta state management in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h`\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3061,"cache_read_input_tokens":75728,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3061},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"878e1e0a-cd22-4ebe-8842-6228d4179c05","uuid":"c8c28152-b33c-4313-8859-11ba890a619d"}

Line 24-28: Constructor takes GrpcMux, callbacks, resource decoder, stats, and type_url\\n  - Line 40: Calls `grpc_mux_->addWatch()` to register watch with the multiplexer\\n\\n- **gRPC Multiplexer**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h` and `.cc`\\n  - `GrpcMuxImpl`: Manages multiple xDS API streams through a single gRPC connection\\n  - Multiplexes different resource types (LDS, CDS, RDS, EDS) onto the AggregatedDiscoveryService stream\\n  - Handles request batching and response routing\\n\\n- **Updated Multiplexer**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h` and `.cc`\\n  - `NewGrpcMuxImpl`: Extended multiplexer supporting both SOTW and Delta xDS\\n  - Better resource state management and failure handling\\n\\n- **Stream Communication**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream.h`\\n  - `GrpcStream<RequestProto, ResponseProto>`: Template-based bidirectional gRPC stream\\n  - Manages connection establishment, reconnection logic with exponential backoff\\n  - Rate limiting of requests (configurable token bucket)\\n  - Lines 51-70: `establishNewStream()` creates new bidirectional stream to management server\\n  - Line 74: `sendMessage()` sends DiscoveryRequest to server\\n  - Handles both SOTW (`DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse`) and Delta (`DeltaDiscoveryRequest/DeltaDiscoveryResponse`) variants\\n\\n## Configuration Flow Sequence\\n\\n1. **Envoy Startup**: Envoy creates a GrpcSubscriptionImpl for each xDS resource type (listeners, clusters, routes, etc.)\\n2. **Subscription Registration**: GrpcSubscriptionImpl calls `GrpcMux::addWatch()` to register interest in resources\\n3. **Stream Establishment**: GrpcMux creates a GrpcStream that establishes a bidirectional gRPC connection to the management server using the AggregatedDiscoveryService/StreamAggregatedResources RPC\\n4. **Request Sending**: Envoy sends DiscoveryRequest messages containing:\\n   - version_info: Current known version (empty on first request)\\n   - type_url: The resource type being requested (e.g., type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.v3.Listener)\\n   - resource_names: Specific resource names to subscribe to\\n   - response_nonce: For ACK/NACK responses\\n5. **Server Processing**: The control plane server (go-control-plane) receives the request in StreamAggregatedResources() handler\\n6. **Response Sending**: Server sends DiscoveryResponse with:\\n   - version_info: New configuration version\\n   - resources: Serialized protobuf resources\\n   - type_url: Matching the request\\n   - nonce: For pairing with subsequent ACK/NACK\\n7. **Configuration Update**: Envoy processes DiscoveryResponse, validates config, and either ACKs (sends new request with same version_info and nonce) or NACKs (sends error_detail)\\n8. **Stream Lifecycle**: The gRPC stream remains open, allowing push-based updates. If connection fails, GrpcStream automatically reconnects using backoff strategy\\n\\n## Delta xDS Variant\\n\\nFor resource-efficient updates, the Delta xDS variant uses:\\n- `DeltaDiscoveryRequest`: Includes only changed resources and removals\\n- `DeltaDiscoveryResponse`: Includes only delta resources and nonce (required for acknowledgment)\\n- Implemented in parallel infrastructure: `DeltaAggregatedResources` RPC in `ads.proto`\\n- Delta state management in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h`\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
